 If Sidhu resigns from the party after his membership of Rajya Sabha, it would be a big blow for the PM, but as the relationship between Sidhu and BJP was deteriorating, it is not seen as a surprising decision
 is
 vahiin drugs ke badhate kaarobaar or bhrashtachar ke mudde par kejariwal ne buree tarah punjab sarkaar ko gher rakhaa he

 dilli main bijepi ko dhul chataane vaale kejariwal ab punjab main sarkaar banane ke liye edi chotii kaa jor laga rahe hai par kejariwal yah acchhee tarah jaanate hai ki party ke paas punjab main koi bhi aisa cheharaa nahin hai jo prakaash singh badal evam amarinder singh jitna lokapriy ho
 Kejriwal knows that Sidhu is very popular and his relationship with BJP is extremely bad
 isliye kejariwal siddhu par punjab chunaav main daanv khelte nazar aa rahe hai
 For this, Kejriwal and Sidhu were also secretly in contact with each other for the past several months
 lekin rajya sabha sadsyta chhodane se bada sawaal yah he ki kya siddhu kaa bijepi chhodkar aap main shaamil hone kaa faisla sahi he or kya aap ko unhen mukhyamantri ummidavaar ghoshit karne se faaydaa hoga yaa nuksaan ? Sidhu may have been in politics for more than a decade, but during this time, Sidhu has given priority to the world of entertainment more than politics and public service
 vah sansad main bahes karne se zyaada tivi kaaryakramon main thahaake lagaate hue zyaada nazar aae hai
 So, while being an MP from Amritsar many times, the public has put up posters of his disappearance as he was rarely seen there
 iske alaava siddhu ek bebaaq netaa hai or khulkar apane vichaaron ko prakat karte hai
 Therefore, he may have difficulty in keeping pace with Kejriwal because like Modi, Kejriwal also does not allow anyone other than him to run in the party
 vahiin siddhu ne aane vaale kuch saalon main kai tivi sho or sports kaaryakramon ke liye qaraar kar rakhaa he to kya vah siem ummidavaar banane ke baad apane kaaryakramon ko radd karenge ?tippaniyan Sidhu may be a good orator but his history says that he has never been so serious towards politics that the public can trust him for a serious responsibility like CM post
 aap bhale hi siddhu ke party main shaamil hone ko badi raajnneetik kaamayaabi maane par twitor par pratikriya dete hue kai logon ne kaha ki siddhu prachaar ke dauraan vot jutaney ke kaam se zyaada behatar janata kaa manoranjan karne kaa kaam karenge
 If Sidhu does not fulfill his dream of becoming CM by holding the broom of AAP, then perhaps he will be clean bold forever in his political innings
 isliye siddhu kaa bijepi chhod aap main janaa kisi badi chunauti se kam nahin hoga
 The party also blamed Jaitley's defeat on Sidhu
 party ke kai bade netaaon ne chunaav ke baad siddhu par aarope lagaae the ki unhone bataur saansad apane lok sabha kshetra main koi kaam nahin kiya or zyada samay tivi kaaryakramon ko host karne main bitaayaa
 Hence, the public got angry and voted against the BJP
 jetali kii amritsar main haar ke aarope ne siddhu or bijepi ke rishton main aag main ghi daalane kaa kaam kiya
 For the past two years, Sidhu and his wife and former BJP MLA Navjot Kaur have repeatedly targeted the Punjab Chief Minister and his ally Akali Dal in the government
 siddhu dampatti akali dal ke kaamkaaz se naakhush the or kai baar bijepi ke varisht netaaon se isaki shikaayat bhi kii lekin unki har baat ko party ne nazarandaaz kiya
 Sidhu's wife had exposed corruption in his own government in a sting a few months ago
 unhone apni sarkaar par gambhir nishaanaa sadhate hue kaha tha ki punjab main laal batti lagi gaadiyaan drugs supplai kaa kaam karti hai
 In the month of April this year, Navjot Kaur also announced her resignation from the BJP through a Facebook post
 vahiin navjot siddhu ne kuch samay pehle ek tivi channel ko die gaye intervyuu main kaha tha ki punjab kaa mukhyamantri bananaa unka sabase bada sapana he
 Sidhu is well aware that he will never be declared CM candidate in the alliance of Akali and BJP
 punjab main janata kaa rosh jhel rahi akali-bijepi sarkaar kii kathinaaiyaan aam aadmi party ke maidan main utarane ke baad or bad gai hai
 aap's popularity is increasing day by day in Punjab and it is discussed everywhere that AAP, which is contesting in Punjab for the first time, can become the largest party in the state elections
 siddhu aap ke siem ummidavaar ke rup main punjab chunaav main maidan main utarkar apane sapane ko puraa karnaa chaahate hai
 At the same time, Sidhu was made a member of the Rajya Sabha by the party about two and a half months ago at the behest of Prime Minister Narendra Modi in view of the Punjab elections
 piem yah acchhee tarah jaanate the ki punjab main akali-bijepi sarkaar ke khilaaf logon kaa gussa badhata ja rahaa he or agar aise main siddhu ko kinare kiya to sthiti or kharaab ho sakati he
 Sidhu was admitted to the hospital due to deteriorating health a few days ago, even when Prime Minister Modi took his treatment by tweeting
 rajyasabha kii sadsyta ke baad agar siddhu party se bhi istifa dete hai to yah piem ke liye ek bada jhatka hoga par jis tarah siddhu or bijepi ke rishte bigadate chale ja rahe the, us lihaaz se ise kisi haroonges faisle ke rup main nahin dekha ja rahaa he
 At the same time, Kejriwal has surrounded the Punjab government badly on the issue of increasing drug trade and corruption
 punjab kii janata bhi aam aadmi party par bharosa jataati nazar aa rahi he 
 Kejriwal, who has dented the BJP in Delhi, is now pushing his head to form a government in Punjab, but Kejriwal is well aware that the party does not have any face in Punjab which is as popular as Prakash Singh Badal and Amarinder Singh

 kejariwal jaanate hai ki siddhu behad lokapriy hai or bijepi ke saath unke rishte behad karaab hai

 But the bigger question than leaving the Rajya Sabha membership is whether Sidhu's decision to leave BJP and join AAP is right and will you benefit or harm by declaring him as Chief Minister candidate? siddhu bhale hi raajnneeti main ek dashak se bhi zyaada samay se hon lekin is dauraan siddhu ne raajnneeti va jan seva se zyada manoranjan kii duniya ko praathamikta di he
 He has appeared in TV programs more than arguing in Parliament
 isliye kai baar amritsar ke saansad hone ke dauraan janata ne unke laapata hone ke poster lagaae hai kyonki vah vahaan bahut kam hi dekhe jate the
 Apart from this, Sidhu is an outstanding leader and openly expresses his views
 isliye shaayad kejariwal se talmail baitaane main unhen dikkat ho kyonki modi kii tarah kejariwal bhi party main apane alaava kisi or kii chalane nahin dete hai
 At the same time, Sidhu has tied up for many TV shows and sports programs in the coming years, will he cancel his programs after becoming CM candidate? Comments siddhu bhale hi ek achche vaktaa hon par unka itihaas kahata he ki vah raajnneeti ke prati itane gambhir kabhi nahin dikhe ki un par janata siem pad jaisi gambheer zimmedaari ke liye bharosa kar sake
 You may be reacting on Twitter to Sidhu's inclusion in the party as a huge political feat, and many people said that Sidhu would do better to entertain the public than to raise votes during campaigning
 siddhu agar aap kii jhaadu pakad kar apane siem banane ke sapane ko puraa na kar paae to shaayad vah apni raajnneetik pari main hameshaa ke liye clin bold ho jaayenge
 Therefore, Sidhu leaving BJP and joining AAP will not be less than a big challenge
 beete do saalon se siddhu or unki patni va purv bijepi vidhayak navjot cor ne kai baar punjab ke mukhyamantri va sarkaar main apane sahyogi akali dal ko nishane par liya

 siddhu kii patni ne kuch maah purv ek sting kar apni hi sarkaar main ho rahe bhrashtachar ko ujagar kiya tha

 ) parachute se neeche aane ko bhi kehete hai soft landing7 sitambar ko vikram lander chand kii sataha par utregakarib 45 ghante baad bhartiya antariksh anusandhan sanghathan (ISRO) 7 sitambar ko chandrayan-2 ke vikram lander ko chand ke dakshini dhruv par utaaregaa
 ISRO scientists are calling it soft landing
 bharat pehali baar kisi upgrah par apane kisi yaan kii soft landing karaane ja rahaa he
 If this mission is successful, it will be the fifth country in the world to have this technology
 ye desh hai - america, rus, europe or china
 It will also be the first country to make soft landings with indigenous technology
 aakhirkaar yah soft landing he kya
 
 
 How it is done isamen kya khatra hota he
 What precautions have to be taken? aaie jaanate hai soft landing ke bare main
 
 
 You must have seen that when a man jumps from a ship, after a short height, he opens the parachute and lands
 agar vah parachute na khole to vah gurutvkarshan shakti ke prabhaav or apane vajan kii vajah se teji se jameen par takaraa saktaa he
 This can cause great harm or death to him
 lekin parachute kii vajah se vah soft landing karata he
 The same happens even when the plane lands at an airport
 vimaan kaa payalat pehle pichley pahie ko ranve par land karaata he, phir agle pahie ko
 This makes the weight of the plane come down in the right direction of motion and the landing is safe
 ise bhi soft landing kehete hai
 Former ISRO scientist Vinod Kumar Srivastava said that a man jumping from a parachute and landing of a plane is a good example of a soft landing
 dharti par gurutvkarshan, gati or vajan kii vajah se sef or soft landing ke liye kai upaay hai
 The parachute reduces the weight of a man jumping from the sky and the effect of gravity
 vahiin, plane kii landing ke samay uske wings kaa ek hissaa hawa ko upar kii taraf ho jaataa he taaki hawa ke gharshan se gati ko kam kar sake
 Vinod Kumar Srivastava said that the gravitational power on the moon is less than 1 / 6 of that of the Earth
 yani vahaan girane kii gati bad jaaegi
 There is no atmosphere, so you cannot even exercise to reduce the speed of friction
 yani na to parachute kaa upyog kar sakate hai na hi plane kii tarah landing
 The Vikram lander is moving around the moon at a speed of 2 km per second
 yani 7200 kimi prati ghanta
 At this speed, he cannot land on the surface of the moon
 kyonki vahaan iske takaraane ke impact ko kam karne ke liye koi vyavastha nahin he
 Vinod Kumar Srivastava said that when the Vikram lander starts descending on the lunar surface from a height of 35 km, the five engines below it will be turned on
 jo ingine abhi tak vikram lander ko aage badhaane kaa kaam kar rahaa the, ab vahiin ingine vipareet disha main dabaav banaakar vikram kii gati ko kam karke 2 meter prati second par le aaenge
 The speed will be reduced to a few seconds before landing
 isse vikram lander apane chaaron pairon ke sahare aaraam se neeche utrega
 All this work will be done by the onboard computer present in Vikram
 usamen lage sensors sahi or samtal jagah kii talash karenge, phir vikram kii landing hogi
